vpō helme alēbick ſet named diſtillacio ꝑ balneū marie diſtillacio duplovaſe ſecond maner ſeconde way ye ſhall put ſame water glas ſtandeth horſe downge thā ſhall named diſtillacio per ventrem arenam fyfte maner ſeconde way ye ſhall ſet boldely glas vpō fyre nothyng betweyn fyre onely yron grate yron treuet named diſtillacio per ignem thus yr haue maners ii wayes dyſtyllacyons coſt coſt
